<div>&lt;div id=&quot;eaembedcodecontentcustom&quot;&gt;&lt;link rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot; type=&quot;text/css&quot; href=&quot;/resource/INFAKBResource/css/bootstrap-ea.css&quot; onload=&quot;fnDoKBCssRefresh(this);&quot;/&gt;&lt;style type=&quot;text/css&quot;&gt;.expert-question{color:#0069aa}.collapsing {-webkit-transition: none;transition: none;}&lt;/style&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;container&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;masthead&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;row&quot; style=&quot;padding:10px 20px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-left&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-right&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse in&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Upgrade Planner for Informatica 10.0&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Informatica Upgrade Planner has been designed and created by the Informatica Global Customer Support team to provide an insight into the Informatica product upgrades.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;This interactive self-service guide provides the information required to upgrade to Informatica 10.0 version from earlier versions. In this guide, you will learn:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New features, architectural changes and steps to upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Different types of upgrade and best practices to follow during the upgrade      cycle&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The upgrade process consists of the following phases:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Perform      the pre-upgrade tasks/checklists&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade      the Informatica Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade      the Repository Service Contents&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade      the Informatica Client Tools&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Perform      the post-upgrade tasks&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The upgrade steps may involve additional steps based on the version you are upgrading from. To start with the upgrade, let us understand your existing implementation. This step-by-step process can be used for upgrading to Informatica version 10 from the earlier versions.&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;It is always recommended to run the upgrade on a development environment before upgrading the production.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select your existing Informatica version...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#d6d1e410-7d30-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#e695d2d0-7d12-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backd6d1e410-7d30-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#e695d2d0-7d12-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Team based development and version control support for IDQ Model Repository Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Big Data Management Configuration Utility to automate part of the configuration process for Big Data Management.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary for Email Notification, Approval Workflow and Import/Export.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Informatica Admin Console for Bird&amp;rsquo;s eye view of the Domain and Service health and Monitor progress of Jobs in detail.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New Profile UI and Visualizations. Features to compare the historical profile run and outlier detection.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Support for profiling on XML/JSON file and scorecard filters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dynamic mappings to change sources, targets, and transformation logic at run time based on parameters and rules that you define.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Native Connectivity to Microsoft SQL Server from UNIX machines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Major enhancements on parameterization in Mercury for better re-usability of the artifacts. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Partitioning support in Mercury platform.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Application Services pre-upgrade checklist&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the Application Services, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure POSIX Asynchronous I/O: If you install Informatica on IBM AIX, make POSIX Asynchronous I/O&amp;nbsp;available on any node where you want to.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Informatica Environment Variables:&amp;nbsp;You can configure the INFA_DOMAINS_FILE and INFA_HOME environment variables to store the domain and installation location settings.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Locale Environment Variables:&amp;nbsp;Use LANG, LC_CTYPE, or LC_ALL to set the UNIX code page. Different UNIX operating systems require different values for the same locale. The value for the locale variable is case sensitive. For Oracle database clients, set NLS_LANG to the locale you want the database client and server to use with the login.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the Keystore File Location for the Administrator Tool:&amp;nbsp;If you used a keystore file that you created to secure the connection to the Administrator tool, you must verify the keystore file location before you access the Administrator tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Clear Browser Cache:&amp;nbsp;Before you access the Administrator tool, clear the browser cache. On Windows Internet Explorer, delete the browsing history, including temporary files, cookies, and history.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete Changing the Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;If you chose to change the node configuration during the domain upgrade because you migrated the Informatica services installation to a different machine, you must perform additional tasks before you upgrade the application services.&amp;nbsp;You must perform the following additional tasks:    </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the environment variables.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the range of dynamic port numbers.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the location of the node backup directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the Application Services upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#d0b8bae0-7cf4-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c9a30670-7cfe-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backd0b8bae0-7cf4-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#c9a30670-7cfe-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backc9a30670-7cfe-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c9a30670-7cfe-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c9a30670-7cfe-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;91af7250-7cd9-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#76aff100-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#91af7250-7cd9-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back76aff100-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#91af7250-7cd9-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;You may need to upgrade the domain with or without node configuration change depending on your current and new system requirements. Below are the high level steps for domain upgrade. Refer Informatica 10.0 - upgrading from 9.6.1 guide for complete steps.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade      the Domain:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain of a previous       version of Informatica services. The server installer provides a domain       upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard installs Informatica 10.0 in the installation       directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of       the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard reads the domain information from files in       the previous version and uses the same settings to configure the domain       and server files for Informatica 10.0. It upgrades the tables of the       domain configuration repository in the same database as the previous       version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you start the upgrade. Run       the installer on all machines that host previous versions of Informatica       that you want to upgrade. On Windows, you can upgrade in graphical or       silent mode. On UNIX, you can upgrade in console or silent mode.&lt;br /&gt;Note: In a multi-node domain, upgrade the master gateway node before you upgrade other nodes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade      the Domain with changes to Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;When you upgrade the domain, you       can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node       host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated an Informatica       services installation to a different machine, choose to change the node       configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the node on the new       machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated the domain configuration       repository to a different database, choose to change the node       configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the new database. If the domain configuration repository database       type or version is no longer supported, you must migrate the repository       to a different database. Migrate the repository in the previous       Informatica instance before you upgrade the domain.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before       you run the installer. On Windows, you can run the installer in graphical       or silent mode. On UNIX, you can run the installer in console or silent       mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#7d2dc6b0-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#91af7250-7cd9-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back7d2dc6b0-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#91af7250-7cd9-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;You may need to upgrade the domain with or without node configuration change depending on your current and new system requirements. Below are the high level steps for domain upgrade. Refer Informatica 10.0 - upgrading from 9.6.1 guide for complete steps.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade      the Domain:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain of a previous       version of Informatica services. The server installer provides a domain       upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard installs Informatica 10.0 in the installation       directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of       the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard reads the domain information from files in       the previous version and uses the same settings to configure the domain       and server files for Informatica 10.0. It upgrades the tables of the       domain configuration repository in the same database as the previous       version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you start the upgrade. Run       the installer on all machines that host previous versions of Informatica       that you want to upgrade. On Windows, you can upgrade in graphical or       silent mode. On UNIX, you can upgrade in console or silent mode.&lt;br /&gt;Note: In a multi-node domain, upgrade the master gateway node before you upgrade other nodes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade      the Domain with changes to Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;When you upgrade the domain, you       can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node       host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated an Informatica       services installation to a different machine, choose to change the node       configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the node on the new       machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated the domain configuration       repository to a different database, choose to change the node       configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the new database. If the domain configuration repository database       type or version is no longer supported, you must migrate the repository       to a different database. Migrate the repository in the previous       Informatica instance before you upgrade the domain.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before       you run the installer. On Windows, you can run the installer in graphical       or silent mode. On UNIX, you can run the installer in console or silent       mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;div class=&quot;WordSection1&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;Informatica platform consists of a server component and one or more client components. Informatica provides separate installers to upgrade the Informatica services and clients.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;If the product version that is currently installed cannot be upgraded to Informatica 10.0, you must first upgrade to a supported version. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;GramE&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;To determine the Informatica product version that is currently installed, click &lt;em&gt;Help &amp;gt; About Informatica Administrator&lt;/em&gt; in the Informatica Administrator Console header area.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;The following table describes the Informatica product versions from which you can upgrade:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;In the Informatica Administrator header area, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&amp;nbsp;&amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Select the objects to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Alternatively, specify if you want to Automatically recycle services after upgrade. If you want to automatically recycle services after upgrade, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard restarts the services after they have been upgraded.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;If the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;errors exist, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;dialog box appears. Review the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Resolve the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Enter the repository login information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, select the option to use the same login information for all repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard upgrades each service and displays the status and processing details.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;When the upgrade completes, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Summary&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;section displays the list of services and their upgrade status.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Click each service to view the upgrade details in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Details&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;section. Alternatively, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Report&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;to save the upgrade details to a file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you do not want to save the report, click&lt;em&gt;&amp;nbsp;Save Previous Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;the next time you launch the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Close&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;If you did not select to automatically recycle services after upgrade, restart the upgraded services.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view post IDQ Service upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span&gt;Minimum Requirements&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Team based development and version control support for IDQ Model Repository Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary for Email Notification, Approval Workflow and Import/Export.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Informatica Admin Console for Bird&amp;rsquo;s eye view of the Domain and Service health and Monitor progress of Jobs in detail.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New Profile UI and Visualizations. Features to compare the historical profile run and outlier detection.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Support for profiling on XML/JSON file and scorecard filters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dynamic mappings to change sources, targets, and transformation logic at run time based on parameters and rules that you define.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Native Connectivity to Microsoft SQL Server from UNIX machines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Major enhancements on parameterization in Mercury for better re-usability of the artifacts.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Partitioning support in Mercury platform.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary for Email Notification, Approval Workflow and Import/Export.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Informatica Admin Console for Bird&amp;rsquo;s eye view of the Domain and Service health and Monitor progress of Jobs in detail.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New Profile UI and Visualizations. Features to compare the historical profile run and outlier detection.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Support for profiling on XML/JSON file and scorecard filters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dynamic mappings to change sources, targets, and transformation logic at run time based on parameters and rules that you define.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Native Connectivity to Microsoft SQL Server from UNIX machines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Major enhancements on parameterization in Mercury for better re-usability of the artifacts. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Partitioning support in Mercury platform.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;To upgrade Informatica, complete the following pre-installation tasks before starting the upgrade:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;For step by step process for each step, refer the &lt;a title=&quot;PowerCenter Document Set for 10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/PowerCenter-10.0-EN.zip&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrading from 9.6.1 Guide&lt;/a&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific Hardware/Software/Patch requirement for Application services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Configure Environment Variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the Temporary files, Code Pages etc.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the Domain&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;-&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Back up the domain configuration database and the metadata configuration files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the repositories for upgrade:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Backup the repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Stop the services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;This applies to Reporting Service, Metadata Manager Service, and Model Repository Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt; &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the Reporting and Dashboards Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare Profile Warehouse, Reference Data Warehouse/Directories, Staging and Human Task Databases.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Clear the environment variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the previous installation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Stop Informatica Services&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#9acecde0-7cd9-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#1090ef00-7cca-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back9acecde0-7cd9-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#1090ef00-7cca-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;To upgrade Informatica, complete the following pre-installation tasks before starting the upgrade:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;For step by step process for each step, refer the &lt;a title=&quot;PowerCenter Document Set for 10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/PowerCenter-10.0-EN.zip&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrading from 9.6.1 Guide&lt;/a&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific Hardware/Software/Patch requirement for Application services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Configure Environment Variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the Temporary files, Code Pages etc.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the Domain&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;-&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Back up the domain configuration database and the metadata configuration files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the repositories for upgrade:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Backup the repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Stop the services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;This applies to Reporting Service, Metadata Manager Service, and Model Repository Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt; &lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Stop Informatica Services&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back1090ef00-7cca-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#1090ef00-7cca-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#1090ef00-7cca-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;0e4ef800-7cfb-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Pointers to consider while upgrading to Informatica 10.0 from 9.6.1 or Prior Version&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are some of the points to consider while upgrading to Informatica 10.0 from 9.6.1 or Prior:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While performing the backup/restore steps, the post-upgrade user will lose&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;PCSF_RUN_LOG&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and the licensing information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While installing 10.0 fresh or while upgrading to 10.0, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;keyword&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;input is required from the user. This replaces the generic encryption key (delivered with the product) &amp;nbsp;to encrypt passwords within the server environment. This is a mandatory step and is not dependent on whether SSL/Kerberos is being used.&amp;nbsp; &lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Make sure you save the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;keyword&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;entered during the upgrade or fresh install so that even if the encryption key is&amp;nbsp;lost, it could be re-generated using the keyword.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While upgrading the domain, the log events directory points to the location you specified in the previous version. While upgrading the domain with changes to the node configuration, the log events directory points to the isp/logs directory in the new installation directory. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To use a different directory for the logs, update the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Log Directory Path&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;property for the domain in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Administrator&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;tool. You can also use&lt;em&gt;&amp;nbsp;infasetup updateGatewaynode&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;to update the directory.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;For example, you can configure the log events directory as the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;server/infa_shared/logs&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory in the new installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the Advance Upgrade options in Informatica 10.0?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#40d9a8c0-7c37-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a463a4a0-7c36-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back40d9a8c0-7c37-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#a463a4a0-7c36-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Team based development and version control support for IDQ Model Repository Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Big Data Management Configuration Utility to automate part of the configuration process for Big Data Management.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary for Email Notification, Approval Workflow and Import/Export.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Informatica Admin Console for Bird&amp;rsquo;s eye view of the Domain and Service health and Monitor progress of Jobs in detail.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New Profile UI and Visualizations. Features to compare the historical profile run and outlier detection.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Support for profiling on XML/JSON file and scorecard filters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dynamic mappings to change sources, targets, and transformation logic at run time based on parameters and rules that you define.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Native Connectivity to Microsoft SQL Server from UNIX machines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Major enhancements on parameterization in Mercury for better re-usability of the artifacts. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Partitioning support in Mercury platform.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#48420580-7c37-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a463a4a0-7c36-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back48420580-7c37-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#a463a4a0-7c36-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Team based development and version control support for IDQ Model Repository Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary for Email Notification, Approval Workflow and Import/Export.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Informatica Admin Console for Bird&amp;rsquo;s eye view of the Domain and Service health and Monitor progress of Jobs in detail.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Dynamic mappings to change sources, targets, and transformation logic at run time based on parameters and rules that you define.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Native Connectivity to Microsoft SQL Server from UNIX machines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

href=&quot;#932e7af0-7d0a-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#b9f61230-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back932e7af0-7d0a-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#b9f61230-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;To run the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;In the Informatica Administrator header area, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&amp;nbsp;&amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Select the objects to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Alternatively, specify if you want to Automatically recycle services after upgrade. If you want to automatically recycle services after upgrade, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard restarts the services after they have been upgraded.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;If the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;errors exist, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;dialog box appears. Review the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Resolve the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Enter the repository login information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, select the option to use the same login information for all repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard upgrades each service and displays the status and processing details.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;When the upgrade completes, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Summary&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;section displays the list of services and their upgrade status.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Click each service to view the upgrade details in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Details&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;section. Alternatively, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Report&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;to save the upgrade details to a file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you do not want to save the report, click&lt;em&gt;&amp;nbsp;Save Previous Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;the next time you launch the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Close&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;If you did not select to automatically recycle services after upgrade, restart the upgraded services.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backb9f61230-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#b9f61230-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#b9f61230-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;d7561f00-7c0e-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New features/enhancements with Informatica version 10.0&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Team based development and version control support for IDQ Model Repository Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Big Data Management Configuration Utility to automate part of the configuration process for Big Data Management.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary for Email Notification, Approval Workflow and Import/Export.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Informatica Admin Console for Bird&amp;rsquo;s eye view of the Domain and Service health and Monitor progress of Jobs in detail.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New Profile UI and Visualizations. Features to compare the historical profile run and outlier detection.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Support for profiling on XML/JSON file and scorecard filters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dynamic mappings to change sources, targets, and transformation logic at run time based on parameters and rules that you define.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Native Connectivity to Microsoft SQL Server from UNIX machines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Major enhancements on parameterization in Mercury for better re-usability of the artifacts.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Partitioning support in Mercury platform.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For information on new features with Informatica 9.6.1 refer &lt;a title=&quot;Informatica - 9.6.1 - New Features Guide - (English)&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_961_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1&amp;nbsp;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the prerequisites for the upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check the latest service pack release of Informatica 10.0 while raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to check Product Availability Matrix (PAM) for 10.0?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Pre-installation Tasks&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;To upgrade Informatica, complete the following pre-installation tasks before starting the upgrade:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;For step by step process for each step, refer the &lt;a title=&quot;PowerCenter Document Set for 10.0&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/PowerCenter-10.0-EN.zip&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Upgrading from 9.6.1 Guide&lt;/a&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific Hardware/Software/Patch requirement for Application services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Configure Environment Variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the Temporary files, Code Pages etc.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the Domain&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;-&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Back up the domain configuration database and the metadata configuration files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Prepare the repositories for upgrade:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Backup the repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;Stop the services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;This applies to Reporting Service, Metadata Manager Service, and Model Repository Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt; &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the Reporting and Dashboards Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare Profile Warehouse, Reference Data Warehouse/Directories, Staging and Human Task Databases.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Clear the environment variables&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;for the previous installation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font3&quot;&gt;Stop Informatica Services&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text265Font2&quot;&gt;on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the Domain upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;IDQ Services - Post Upgrade Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;IDQ Upgrade from 9.6.1 to 10.0&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Perform the post-upgrade tasks for the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Data Integration Service:&amp;nbsp;Verify the Human task database settings&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;Content Management Service: Verify the Location Identity Population files, Restart service&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Analyst Service: Verify Flat File Cache Location, Verify Human Task Properties and Restart Service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Reference Data:&amp;nbsp;After you upgrade, complete the post-upgrade tasks for reference data objects and files.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiles:&amp;nbsp;Migrate Profile and Scorecard Results and Import Data Domains&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;IDQ Upgrade from 9.5.1 to 10.0&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Perform the post-upgrade tasks for the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;Data integration Service: Verify the Human task database settings&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;Content Management Service: Verify the Location Identity Population files, Restart service&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;Analyst Service: The Data Director Service is converted to an Analyst Service. You may view two Analyst Services when the upgrade is complete.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;Verify the Human Task Properties&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you upgrade a domain that includes a Data Director Service, the upgrade operation converts the Data Director Service to an Analyst Service. The Analyst Service uses the Data Integration Service properties from the Data Director Service to update the Human task properties. Any user who worked on Human task instances in Informatica Data Director for Data Quality can log in to the Analyst Service URL to work on the task instances.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you upgrade services in a domain that contains an Analyst Service and a Data Director Service, the domain contains two Analyst Services when the upgrade operation is complete. You can maintain the two services, or you can merge the properties to a single Analyst Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;Reference Data:&amp;nbsp;After you upgrade, complete the post-upgrade tasks for reference data objects and files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3921Font1&quot;&gt;Profiles:&amp;nbsp;Migrate Profile and Scorecard Results and Import Data Domains.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Team based development and version control support for IDQ Model Repository Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Big Data Management Configuration Utility to automate part of the configuration process for Big Data Management.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary for Email Notification, Approval Workflow and Import/Export.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Informatica Admin Console for Bird&amp;rsquo;s eye view of the Domain and Service health and Monitor progress of Jobs in detail.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New Profile UI and Visualizations. Features to compare the historical profile run and outlier detection.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt; Support for profiling on XML/JSON file and scorecard filters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dynamic mappings to change sources, targets, and transformation logic at run time based on parameters and rules that you define.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Native Connectivity to Microsoft SQL Server from UNIX machines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Major enhancements on parameterization in Mercury for better re-usability of the artifacts. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Partitioning support in Mercury platform.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#d7a0f4c0-7c3c-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#d6d1e410-7d30-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backd7a0f4c0-7c3c-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#d6d1e410-7d30-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the prerequisites:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check the latest service pack release of Informatica 10.0 while raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backd6d1e410-7d30-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#d6d1e410-7d30-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#d6d1e410-7d30-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;6e8a8c30-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Post-installation Verification and Adding Kerberos Authentication Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;To configure Kerberos authentication for the Informatica domain at the command prompt, do the following steps:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the upgrade was successful and the upgraded domain is working appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify the Kerberos configuration and copy the configuration file to the Informatica directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Create the SPNs and keytab files that are required by the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Configure the Kerberos authentication for the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the nodes in the Informatica domain - Run &lt;em&gt;infasetup updategatewaynode/updateworkernode&lt;/em&gt; commands to update all gateway and worker nodes in the domain with Kerberos authentication server information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the client machines -&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Copy the Kerberos configuration file and set the environment variable on the machines that host the Informatica clients.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Start the Informatica domain and verify if that the domain runs with the Kerberos authentication appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font2&quot;&gt;Note&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;The steps provided are based on the assumption that you have upgraded the Informatica services and clients successfully. Verify if the upgrade is complete before configuring the domain to use the Kerberos network authentication.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Kerberos authentication is optional and is disabled by default.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;After the Kerberos authentication is enabled for the domain, it cannot be disabled. After the Kerberos authentication is enabled, the native users are disabled and only the Kerberos users can be authenticated.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;For more information refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;PowerCenter Document Set for 10.0 (English)&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/PowerCenter-10.0-EN.zip&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica 10.0 &amp;ndash; upgrading from 9.6.1&lt;/a&gt; &amp;gt; &quot;Chapter 10: After you upgrade&amp;rdquo; in this section.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the pointers to consider for the upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back9f84b730-7d0d-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#9f84b730-7d0d-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#9f84b730-7d0d-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;11fbe880-7cfd-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Domain Pre-upgrade Checklist&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the domain and server files, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific requirements. Review the prerequisites and environment variable configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall Informatica B2B Data Transformation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the domain. Back up the domain and verify database user account permissions.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the PowerCenter repository. Back up the PowerCenter repository.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Export the Jaspersoft resource.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare Metadata Manager:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata Manager warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Export, purge, and delete business glossaries&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the Metadata Manager service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata Manager properties file&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the Data Analyzer repository.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Assign roles to users and groups.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Data Analyzer repository.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify database user account requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you are using IDQ services, review IDQ services upgrade process before starting the upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Shut down the domain.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;You must shut down the domain before you upgrading. To shut down the domain, stop the Informatica service process on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Run the Pre-installation (i10Pi) System Check Tool to verify whether the machine meets the system requirements for installation or upgrade.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare to change the node configuration. Complete the additional pre-upgrade tasks if you want to change the node configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review the operating system specific requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the keystore file name and location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Domain and Server Files Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain and server files. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The upgrade wizard installs the Informatica files in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the Domain upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Manage&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3292&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3292anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font0&quot;&gt;Before y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;ou upgrade the Domain and Server files, perform the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.5.1 or 9.6.1 to IDQ 10.0&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the following:     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Model Repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiling Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Reference Data Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Staging Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Human Task Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#b9f61230-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#906c98a0-7d06-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backb9f61230-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#906c98a0-7d06-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3909Font1&quot;&gt;Use the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard to upgrade services from IDQ 9.5.1 or 9.6.1 to Informatica DQ 10.0. The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard provides the following options:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade multiple services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable services before the upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Display upgraded services in a list along with services that require an upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Manage&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3292&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3292anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font0&quot;&gt;Before y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;ou upgrade the Domain and Server files, perform the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.5.1 or 9.6.1 to IDQ 10.0&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the following:     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Model Repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiling Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Reference Data Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Staging Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Human Task Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back906c98a0-7d06-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#906c98a0-7d06-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#906c98a0-7d06-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c5fe9390-7c0e-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New features/enhancements with Informatica version 10.0&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Team based development and version control support for IDQ Model Repository Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Big Data Management Configuration Utility to automate part of the configuration process for Big Data Management.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary for Email Notification, Approval Workflow and Import/Export.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Informatica Admin Console for Bird&amp;rsquo;s eye view of the Domain and Service health and Monitor progress of Jobs in detail.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New Profile UI and Visualizations. Features to compare the historical profile run and outlier detection.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Support for profiling on XML/JSON file and scorecard filters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dynamic mappings to change sources, targets, and transformation logic at run time based on parameters and rules that you define.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Native Connectivity to Microsoft SQL Server from UNIX machines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Major enhancements on parameterization in Mercury for better re-usability of the artifacts. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Partitioning support in Mercury platform.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;div class=&quot;WordSection1&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;Informatica platform consists of a server component and one or more client components. Informatica provides separate installers to upgrade the Informatica services and clients.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;If the product version that is currently installed cannot be upgraded to Informatica 10.0, you must first upgrade to a supported version. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;GramE&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;To determine the Informatica product version that is currently installed, click &lt;em&gt;Help &amp;gt; About Informatica Administrator&lt;/em&gt; in the Informatica Administrator Console header area.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;The following table describes the Informatica product versions from which you can upgrade:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;td width=&quot;192&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
