style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Upgrade to version 9.6.1, and then upgrade to upgrade to version 10.0.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For information on upgrading to Informatica 9.6.1, refer to the upgrade planner for&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;9.6.1 Upgrade Planner&quot; href=&quot;../conversation/?id=44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;9.6.1 upgrade&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back338628f0-7c01-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#338628f0-7c01-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#338628f0-7c01-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;7d2dc6b0-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;No, Show me Application Service pre-upgrade checklist. &lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#f2192620-7cfe-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#7d2dc6b0-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backf2192620-7cfe-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#7d2dc6b0-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the Application Services, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure POSIX Asynchronous I/O: If you install Informatica on IBM AIX, make POSIX Asynchronous I/O&amp;nbsp;available on any node where you want to.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Informatica Environment Variables:&amp;nbsp;You can configure the INFA_DOMAINS_FILE and INFA_HOME environment variables to store the domain and installation location settings.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure Locale Environment Variables:&amp;nbsp;Use LANG, LC_CTYPE, or LC_ALL to set the UNIX code page. Different UNIX operating systems require different values for the same locale. The value for the locale variable is case sensitive. For Oracle database clients, set NLS_LANG to the locale you want the database client and server to use with the login.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the Keystore File Location for the Administrator Tool:&amp;nbsp;If you used a keystore file that you created to secure the connection to the Administrator tool, you must verify the keystore file location before you access the Administrator tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Clear Browser Cache:&amp;nbsp;Before you access the Administrator tool, clear the browser cache. On Windows Internet Explorer, delete the browsing history, including temporary files, cookies, and history.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete Changing the Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;If you chose to change the node configuration during the domain upgrade because you migrated the Informatica services installation to a different machine, you must perform additional tasks before you upgrade the application services.&amp;nbsp;You must perform the following additional tasks:    </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the environment variables.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the range of dynamic port numbers.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the location of the node backup directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back7d2dc6b0-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#7d2dc6b0-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#7d2dc6b0-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;3862b590-7d10-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Team based development and version control support for IDQ Model Repository Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Big Data Management Configuration Utility to automate part of the configuration process for Big Data Management.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary for Email Notification, Approval Workflow and Import/Export.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Informatica Admin Console for Bird&amp;rsquo;s eye view of the Domain and Service health and Monitor progress of Jobs in detail.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New Profile UI and Visualizations. Features to compare the historical profile run and outlier detection.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt; Support for profiling on XML/JSON file and scorecard filters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dynamic mappings to change sources, targets, and transformation logic at run time based on parameters and rules that you define.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Native Connectivity to Microsoft SQL Server from UNIX machines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Major enhancements on parameterization in Mercury for better re-usability of the artifacts. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Partitioning support in Mercury platform.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For complete details on the new features with Informatica v10 refer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/IN_100_NewFeaturesGuide_en.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;New Features Guide&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the prerequisites for the upgrade?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4916Font1&quot;&gt;If you plan a hardware or database upgrade while upgrading Informatica products, Informatica 10.0 has the capability to support the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a node that runs on an unsupported Operating System.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a clone of a production domain (without altering the production environment)&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;Use the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;em&gt;Allow changes to the Node Host Name and Port Number&lt;/em&gt; option&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;during the Upgrade Directory installation, to make the following key changes to the domain configuration:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Node Host Name and Port Number&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain Database Connection&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To use the advanced options before upgrading, perform the following manual steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Host     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires copying a few configuration files to the new machine before upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Database     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires a backup and restore of domain to a new database instance before upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;72cb9ad0-7d06-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#11ebbae0-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#72cb9ad0-7d06-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back11ebbae0-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#72cb9ad0-7d06-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3197Font1&quot;&gt;Use the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard to upgrade services IDS 9.5.1 and 9.6.1 to Informatica DS 10.0. The service upgrade wizard provides the following options:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade multiple services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable services before the upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Display upgraded services in a list along with services that require an upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Manage&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3225&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3225anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;In the Informatica Administrator header area, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&amp;nbsp;&amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Select the objects to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Alternatively, specify if you want to Automatically recycle services after upgrade. If you want to automatically recycle services after upgrade, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard restarts the services after they have been upgraded.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;If dependency errors exist, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;dialog box appears. Review the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Resolve the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Enter the repository login information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, select to use the same login information for all repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;-&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard upgrades each service and displays the status and processing details.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;When the upgrade completes, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Summary&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;section displays the list of services and their upgrade status -&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;Click each service to view the upgrade details in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Details &lt;/em&gt;section.&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;to save the upgrade details to a file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you do not want to save the report, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Previous Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;the next time you launch the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;wizard.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Close&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;If you select not to automatically recycle services after an upgrade,&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;restart the upgraded services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;SQL Data Services Drivers&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After upgrading Informatica Data Services, upgrade the Informatica JDBC or ODBC Drivers for SQL Data Services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3300&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3300Font1&quot;&gt;To upgrade the driver, run the Informatica JDBC/ODBC driver installation program and select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;option.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#2d9b0330-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#f2192620-7cfe-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back2d9b0330-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#f2192620-7cfe-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Application Service Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The Informatica services version that you upgrade from determines the application service upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Some Informatica services versions require that you upgrade the application services. When you upgrade an application service, you must also upgrade the dependent services. When you upgrade an application service, the upgrade process upgrades the database contents of the databases associated with the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the service upgrade wizard, the &lt;em&gt;Actions &lt;/em&gt;menu of each service, or the command line to upgrade application services. The Service Upgrade wizard upgrades multiple services in the appropriate order and checks for dependencies. If you use the Actions menu of each service or the command line to upgrade application services, you must upgrade the application services in the correct order and verify that you upgrade dependent services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The privileges required to upgrade application services depend on the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After you upgrade the Model Repository Service, check the log to verify that the upgrade completed successfully.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Administrator.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt;, and select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;The Service Upgrade wizard displays upgraded services in a list along with services and associated databases that require an upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Select the application services that you want to upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrade the Client&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the client installer to upgrade a previous version of the Informatica client tools. The Informatica client tools are installed on the installation directory you specify. The client installer configures the newly installed client tools with the same settings as the previous version. The client installer does not modify the files of the previous version of the client tools.&amp;nbsp;You can upgrade the Informatica client tools either in Graphical Mode or Silent Mode.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; <div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check the latest service pack release of Informatica 10.0 while raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back41f915e0-7d10-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#41f915e0-7d10-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#41f915e0-7d10-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;f82aa250-7c36-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New Major Features/Enhancements with Informatica 10.0 Release&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with Informatica 10.0:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Team based development and version control support for IDQ Model Repository Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Big Data Management Configuration Utility to automate part of the configuration process for Big Data Management.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Business Glossary for Email Notification, Approval Workflow and Import/Export.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to command line programs.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Informatica Admin Console for Bird&amp;rsquo;s eye view of the Domain and Service health and Monitor progress of Jobs in detail.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New Profile UI and Visualizations. Features to compare the historical profile run and outlier detection.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Support for profiling on XML/JSON file and scorecard filters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dynamic mappings to change sources, targets, and transformation logic at run time based on parameters and rules that you define.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to Metadata Manager.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Various enhancements to PowerExchange Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Native Connectivity to Microsoft SQL Server from UNIX machines.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Major enhancements on parameterization in Mercury for better re-usability of the artifacts. &lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Partitioning support in Mercury platform.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#72cb9ad0-7d06-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a3300260-7d01-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back72cb9ad0-7d06-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#a3300260-7d01-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;After upgrading the domain, server files, application services, and client files, complete the following post upgrade tasks:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure LDAP connectivity.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;The default maximum size for user import is set to 1000. Increase the value if you have more than 1000 users.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update ODBC data sources. The Informatica installation includes new DataDirect ODBC drivers. Re-create each ODBC data source to use the new drivers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the log events directory is appropriate. To use a different directory for the logs, update the Log Directory Path property for the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;If you exported business glossaries from Metadata Manager, import the glossaries into the Analyst tool.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Complete the following post upgrade tasks for each Metadata Manager Service:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the &lt;em&gt;Metadata Manager&lt;/em&gt; properties file to include any customization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create business glossary resources based on the business glossaries that you imported into the Analyst tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall and reinstall the Metadata Manager Agent after configuring the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update the Reporting and Dashboards Service properties file and upgrade to Jaspersoft 4.2.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify Keystore and Truststore File Locations:&amp;nbsp;If you used a custom SSL certificate to enable secure communication in the previous domain, you must verify the keystore and truststore file locations after you upgrade. The upgrade process does not update these locations. If used default Informatica SSL in previous version, then no need to verify.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure a Secure Database: You can optionally configure the domain configuration repository on a database that is secured with the SSL protocol.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review IDQ related services after the upgrade to make sure they are up and running.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#906c98a0-7d06-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a3300260-7d01-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back906c98a0-7d06-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#a3300260-7d01-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;After upgrading the domain, server files, application services, and client files, complete the following post upgrade tasks:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure LDAP connectivity.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;The default maximum size for user import is set to 1000. Increase the value if you have more than 1000 users.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update ODBC data sources. The Informatica installation includes new DataDirect ODBC drivers. Re-create each ODBC data source to use the new drivers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the log events directory is appropriate. To use a different directory for the logs, update the Log Directory Path property for the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;If you exported business glossaries from Metadata Manager, import the glossaries into the Analyst tool.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Complete the following post upgrade tasks for each Metadata Manager Service:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the &lt;em&gt;Metadata Manager&lt;/em&gt; properties file to include any customization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create business glossary resources based on the business glossaries that you imported into the Analyst tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall and reinstall the Metadata Manager Agent after configuring the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update the Reporting and Dashboards Service properties file and upgrade to Jaspersoft 4.2.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify Keystore and Truststore File Locations:&amp;nbsp;If you used a custom SSL certificate to enable secure communication in the previous domain, you must verify the keystore and truststore file locations after you upgrade. The upgrade process does not update these locations. If used default Informatica SSL in previous version, then no need to verify.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure a Secure Database: You can optionally configure the domain configuration repository on a database that is secured with the SSL protocol.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review IDQ related services after the upgrade to make sure they are up and running.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;4083d470-7ce3-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Domain Upgrade Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;You may need to upgrade the domain with or without node configuration change depending on your current and new system requirements. Below are the high level steps for domain upgrade. Refer Informatica 10.0 - upgrading from 9.6.1 guide for complete steps.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade      the Domain:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain of a previous       version of Informatica services. The server installer provides a domain       upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard installs Informatica 10.0 in the installation       directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of       the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard reads the domain information from files in       the previous version and uses the same settings to configure the domain       and server files for Informatica 10.0. It upgrades the tables of the       domain configuration repository in the same database as the previous       version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you start the upgrade. Run       the installer on all machines that host previous versions of Informatica       that you want to upgrade. On Windows, you can upgrade in graphical or       silent mode. On UNIX, you can upgrade in console or silent mode.&lt;br /&gt;Note: In a multi-node domain, upgrade the master gateway node before you upgrade other nodes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade      the Domain with changes to Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;When you upgrade the domain, you       can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node       host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated an Informatica       services installation to a different machine, choose to change the node       configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the node on the new       machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated the domain configuration       repository to a different database, choose to change the node       configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the new database. If the domain configuration repository database       type or version is no longer supported, you must migrate the repository       to a different database. Migrate the repository in the previous       Informatica instance before you upgrade the domain.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before       you run the installer. On Windows, you can run the installer in graphical       or silent mode. On UNIX, you can run the installer in console or silent       mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the Application Services upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#2d9b0330-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#76aff100-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back2d9b0330-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#76aff100-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Application Service Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The Informatica services version that you upgrade from determines the application service upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Some Informatica services versions require that you upgrade the application services. When you upgrade an application service, you must also upgrade the dependent services. When you upgrade an application service, the upgrade process upgrades the database contents of the databases associated with the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the service upgrade wizard, the &lt;em&gt;Actions &lt;/em&gt;menu of each service, or the command line to upgrade application services. The Service Upgrade wizard upgrades multiple services in the appropriate order and checks for dependencies. If you use the Actions menu of each service or the command line to upgrade application services, you must upgrade the application services in the correct order and verify that you upgrade dependent services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The privileges required to upgrade application services depend on the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After you upgrade the Model Repository Service, check the log to verify that the upgrade completed successfully.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Administrator.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt;, and select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;The Service Upgrade wizard displays upgraded services in a list along with services and associated databases that require an upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Select the application services that you want to upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrade the Client&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the client installer to upgrade a previous version of the Informatica client tools. The Informatica client tools are installed on the installation directory you specify. The client installer configures the newly installed client tools with the same settings as the previous version. The client installer does not modify the files of the previous version of the client tools.&amp;nbsp;You can upgrade the Informatica client tools either in Graphical Mode or Silent Mode.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;2d9b0330-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#759c3d70-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#2d9b0330-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back759c3d70-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#2d9b0330-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;To configure Kerberos authentication for the Informatica domain at the command prompt, do the following steps:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the upgrade was successful and the upgraded domain is working appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify the Kerberos configuration and copy the configuration file to the Informatica directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Create the SPNs and keytab files that are required by the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Configure the Kerberos authentication for the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the nodes in the Informatica domain - Run &lt;em&gt;infasetup updategatewaynode/updateworkernode&lt;/em&gt; commands to update all gateway and worker nodes in the domain with Kerberos authentication server information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the client machines -&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Copy the Kerberos configuration file and set the environment variable on the machines that host the Informatica clients.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Start the Informatica domain and verify if that the domain runs with the Kerberos authentication appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font2&quot;&gt;Note&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;The steps provided are based on the assumption that you have upgraded the Informatica services and clients successfully. Verify if the upgrade is complete before configuring the domain to use the Kerberos network authentication.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Kerberos authentication is optional and is disabled by default.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;After the Kerberos authentication is enabled for the domain, it cannot be disabled. After the Kerberos authentication is enabled, the native users are disabled and only the Kerberos users can be authenticated.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;For more information refer to&amp;nbsp;&lt;a title=&quot;PowerCenter Document Set for 10.0 (English)&quot; href=&quot;https://kb.informatica.com/proddocs/Product%20Documentation/4/PowerCenter-10.0-EN.zip&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica 10.0 &amp;ndash; upgrading from 9.6.1&lt;/a&gt; &amp;gt; &quot;Chapter 10: After you upgrade&amp;rdquo; in this section.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

&quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back9b1d22f0-7c3f-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#9b1d22f0-7c3f-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#76aff100-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#46fdb3b0-7cfd-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back76aff100-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#46fdb3b0-7cfd-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;You may need to upgrade the domain with or without node configuration change depending on your current and new system requirements. Below are the high level steps for domain upgrade. Refer Informatica 10.0 - upgrading from 9.6.1 guide for complete steps.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade      the Domain:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain of a previous       version of Informatica services. The server installer provides a domain       upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard installs Informatica 10.0 in the installation       directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of       the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard reads the domain information from files in       the previous version and uses the same settings to configure the domain       and server files for Informatica 10.0. It upgrades the tables of the       domain configuration repository in the same database as the previous       version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you start the upgrade. Run       the installer on all machines that host previous versions of Informatica       that you want to upgrade. On Windows, you can upgrade in graphical or       silent mode. On UNIX, you can upgrade in console or silent mode.&lt;br /&gt;Note: In a multi-node domain, upgrade the master gateway node before you upgrade other nodes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade      the Domain with changes to Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;When you upgrade the domain, you       can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node       host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated an Informatica       services installation to a different machine, choose to change the node       configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the node on the new       machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated the domain configuration       repository to a different database, choose to change the node       configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the new database. If the domain configuration repository database       type or version is no longer supported, you must migrate the repository       to a different database. Migrate the repository in the previous       Informatica instance before you upgrade the domain.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before       you run the installer. On Windows, you can run the installer in graphical       or silent mode. On UNIX, you can run the installer in console or silent       mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#7d2dc6b0-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#46fdb3b0-7cfd-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back7d2dc6b0-7cf2-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#46fdb3b0-7cfd-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;You may need to upgrade the domain with or without node configuration change depending on your current and new system requirements. Below are the high level steps for domain upgrade. Refer Informatica 10.0 - upgrading from 9.6.1 guide for complete steps.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade      the Domain:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain of a previous       version of Informatica services. The server installer provides a domain       upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard installs Informatica 10.0 in the installation       directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of       the previous version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The upgrade wizard reads the domain information from files in       the previous version and uses the same settings to configure the domain       and server files for Informatica 10.0. It upgrades the tables of the       domain configuration repository in the same database as the previous       version.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before you start the upgrade. Run       the installer on all machines that host previous versions of Informatica       that you want to upgrade. On Windows, you can upgrade in graphical or       silent mode. On UNIX, you can upgrade in console or silent mode.&lt;br /&gt;Note: In a multi-node domain, upgrade the master gateway node before you upgrade other nodes.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Upgrade      the Domain with changes to Node Configuration:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;When you upgrade the domain, you       can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node       host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated an Informatica       services installation to a different machine, choose to change the node       configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the node on the new       machine.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you migrated the domain configuration       repository to a different database, choose to change the node       configuration to upgrade the domain and configure the new database. If the domain configuration repository database       type or version is no longer supported, you must migrate the repository       to a different database. Migrate the repository in the previous       Informatica instance before you upgrade the domain.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the pre-upgrade tasks before       you run the installer. On Windows, you can run the installer in graphical       or silent mode. On UNIX, you can run the installer in console or silent       mode.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Check the latest service pack release of Informatica 10.0 while raising a shipping request.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Electronic Software Download: If you download the Informatica installation files from the Informatica Electronic Software Download (ESD) site, the license key is in an email message from Informatica. Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back40d9a8c0-7c37-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#40d9a8c0-7c37-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#40d9a8c0-7c37-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;d0b8bae0-7cf4-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt; Application Services and Client Upgrade Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Application Service Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The Informatica services version that you upgrade from determines the application service upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Some Informatica services versions require that you upgrade the application services. When you upgrade an application service, you must also upgrade the dependent services. When you upgrade an application service, the upgrade process upgrades the database contents of the databases associated with the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the service upgrade wizard, the &lt;em&gt;Actions &lt;/em&gt;menu of each service, or the command line to upgrade application services. The Service Upgrade wizard upgrades multiple services in the appropriate order and checks for dependencies. If you use the Actions menu of each service or the command line to upgrade application services, you must upgrade the application services in the correct order and verify that you upgrade dependent services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The privileges required to upgrade application services depend on the service.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After you upgrade the Model Repository Service, check the log to verify that the upgrade completed successfully.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Log in to Informatica Administrator.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt;, and select&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;. &lt;br /&gt;The Service Upgrade wizard displays upgraded services in a list along with services and associated databases that require an upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Select the application services that you want to upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrade the Client&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the client installer to upgrade a previous version of the Informatica client tools. The Informatica client tools are installed on the installation directory you specify. The client installer configures the newly installed client tools with the same settings as the previous version. The client installer does not modify the files of the previous version of the client tools.&amp;nbsp;You can upgrade the Informatica client tools either in Graphical Mode or Silent Mode.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the post-upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#6e8a8c30-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#d0b8bae0-7cf4-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back6e8a8c30-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#d0b8bae0-7cf4-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; <div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Manage&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3292&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3292anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font0&quot;&gt;Before y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;ou upgrade the Domain and Server files, perform the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.5.1 or 9.6.1 to IDQ 10.0&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the following:     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Model Repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiling Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Reference Data Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Staging Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Human Task Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;The license key can be obtained in the following ways:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text1483Font1&quot;&gt;Installation DVD: If you receive the Informatica installation files in a DVD, the license key file is included in the Informatica License Key CD.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

Copy the license key file to a directory accessible to the user account that installs the product. Contact Informatica Global Customer Support if you do not have a license key.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; <div>&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Domain and Server files&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Application Services&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Informatica Client&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrading the Domain and Server files&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the domain and server files, run the Informatica server installer and select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;option. The domain upgrade wizard installs the server files and configures the domain. If the domain has multiple nodes, you must upgrade all nodes. When you upgrade each node in the domain, you can choose to change the node configuration to allow changes to the node host name, port numbers, or domain configuration repository database.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Upgrading the Application Services&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;After upgrading the Domain and Server files, log in to the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Administrator tool&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and upgrade the application services. The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard provides a list of all applications that must be upgraded. It upgrades the services based on the order required by the dependent objects.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;No, Show me domain pre-upgrade checklist. &lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#46fdb3b0-7cfd-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#9acecde0-7cd9-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back46fdb3b0-7cfd-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#9acecde0-7cd9-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the domain and server files, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific requirements. Review the prerequisites and environment variable configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall Informatica B2B Data Transformation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the domain. Back up the domain and verify database user account permissions.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the PowerCenter repository. Back up the PowerCenter repository.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Export the Jaspersoft resource.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare Metadata Manager:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata Manager warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Export, purge, and delete business glossaries&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the Metadata Manager service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata Manager properties file&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the Data Analyzer repository.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Assign roles to users and groups.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Data Analyzer repository.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify database user account requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you are using IDQ services, review IDQ services upgrade process before starting the upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Shut down the domain.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;You must shut down the domain before you upgrading. To shut down the domain, stop the Informatica service process on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;Run the Pre-installation (i10Pi) System Check Tool to verify whether the machine meets the system requirements for installation or upgrade.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare to change the node configuration. Complete the additional pre-upgrade tasks if you want to change the node configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review the operating system specific requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the keystore file name and location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Domain and Server Files Upgrade&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the domain and server files. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The upgrade wizard installs the Informatica files in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#28740530-99e9-11e5-8526-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#9acecde0-7cd9-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back28740530-99e9-11e5-8526-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#9acecde0-7cd9-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the domain and server files, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Review the Operating System specific requirements. Review the prerequisites and environment variable configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall Informatica B2B Data Transformation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the domain. Back up the domain and verify database user account permissions.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the PowerCenter repository. Back up the PowerCenter repository.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Export the Jaspersoft resource.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare Metadata Manager:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata Manager warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Export, purge, and delete business glossaries&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the Metadata Manager service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata Manager properties file&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the Data Analyzer repository.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Shut down the domain.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;You must shut down the domain before you upgrading. To shut down the domain, stop the Informatica service process on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare to change the node configuration. Complete the additional pre-upgrade tasks if you want to change the node configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review the operating system specific requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the keystore file name and location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backb3451e90-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#b3451e90-7d08-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#63630f20-7cfb-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#759c3d70-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back63630f20-7cfb-11e5-baa1-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#759c3d70-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are some of the points to consider while upgrading to Informatica 10.0 from 9.6.1 or Prior:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While performing the backup/restore steps, the post-upgrade user will lose&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;PCSF_RUN_LOG&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and the licensing information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While installing 10.0 fresh or while upgrading to 10.0, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;keyword&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;input is required from the user. This replaces the generic encryption key (delivered with the product) &amp;nbsp;to encrypt passwords within the server environment. This is a mandatory step and is not dependent on whether SSL/Kerberos is being used.&amp;nbsp; &lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Make sure you save the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;keyword&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;entered during the upgrade or fresh install so that even if the encryption key is&amp;nbsp;lost, it could be re-generated using the keyword.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While upgrading the domain, the log events directory points to the location you specified in the previous version. While upgrading the domain with changes to the node configuration, the log events directory points to the isp/logs directory in the new installation directory. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To use a different directory for the logs, update the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Log Directory Path&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;property for the domain in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Administrator&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;tool. You can also use&lt;em&gt;&amp;nbsp;infasetup updateGatewaynode&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;to update the directory.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;For example, you can configure the log events directory as the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;server/infa_shared/logs&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;directory in the new installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back759c3d70-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#759c3d70-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#43b5a490-7c00-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#759c3d70-7cfa-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;b90116c0-7cfb-11e5-b92b-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Advance Upgrade Options in Informatica 10.0&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4916Font1&quot;&gt;If you plan a hardware or database upgrade while upgrading Informatica products, Informatica 10.0 has the capability to support the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a node that runs on an unsupported Operating System.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a clone of a production domain (without altering the production environment)&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;Use the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;em&gt;Allow changes to the Node Host Name and Port Number&lt;/em&gt; option&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;during the Upgrade Directory installation, to make the following key changes to the domain configuration:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Node Host Name and Port Number&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain Database Connection&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To use the advanced options before upgrading, perform the following manual steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Host     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires copying a few configuration files to the new machine before upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Database     </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires a backup and restore of domain to a new database instance before upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the post-upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot;
