class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;IDS Upgrade Process&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3197Font1&quot;&gt;Use the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard to upgrade services IDS 9.5.1 and 9.6.1 to Informatica DS 10.0. The service upgrade wizard provides the following options:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade multiple services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable services before the upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Display upgraded services in a list along with services that require an upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Manage&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3225&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3225anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;In the Informatica Administrator header area, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Manage&amp;nbsp;&amp;gt;&amp;nbsp;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Select the objects to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Alternatively, specify if you want to Automatically recycle services after upgrade. If you want to automatically recycle services after upgrade, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard restarts the services after they have been upgraded.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;If dependency errors exist, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;dialog box appears. Review the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Resolve the&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;and click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Enter the repository login information.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, select to use the same login information for all repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;-&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;The&amp;nbsp;&lt;span&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;wizard upgrades each service and displays the status and processing details.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;When the upgrade completes, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Summary&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;section displays the list of services and their upgrade status -&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;Click each service to view the upgrade details in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Details &lt;/em&gt;section.&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;to save the upgrade details to a file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you do not want to save the report, click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Save Previous Report&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;the next time you launch the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;wizard.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Close&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3225Font1&quot;&gt;If you select not to automatically recycle services after an upgrade,&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;restart the upgraded services.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;SQL Data Services Drivers&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;After upgrading Informatica Data Services, upgrade the Informatica JDBC or ODBC Drivers for SQL Data Services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3300&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3300Font1&quot;&gt;To upgrade the driver, run the Informatica JDBC/ODBC driver installation program and select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Upgrade&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;option.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>

&quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa62e5f60-7d2f-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a62e5f60-7d2f-11e5-9d8e-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Post Upgrade Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;After upgrading the domain, server files, application services, and client files, complete the following post upgrade tasks:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure LDAP connectivity.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;The default maximum size for user import is set to 1000. Increase the value if you have more than 1000 users.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update ODBC data sources. The Informatica installation includes new DataDirect ODBC drivers. Re-create each ODBC data source to use the new drivers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the log events directory is appropriate. To use a different directory for the logs, update the Log Directory Path property for the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;If you exported business glossaries from Metadata Manager, import the glossaries into the Analyst tool.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Complete the following post upgrade tasks for each Metadata Manager Service:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the &lt;em&gt;Metadata Manager&lt;/em&gt; properties file to include any customization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create business glossary resources based on the business glossaries that you imported into the Analyst tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall and reinstall the Metadata Manager Agent after configuring the Metadata Manager Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update the Reporting and Dashboards Service properties file and upgrade to Jaspersoft 4.2.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify Keystore and Truststore File Locations:&amp;nbsp;If you used a custom SSL certificate to enable secure communication in the previous domain, you must verify the keystore and truststore file locations after you upgrade. The upgrade process does not update these locations. If used default Informatica SSL in previous version, then no need to verify.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure a Secure Database: You can optionally configure the domain configuration repository on a database that is secured with the SSL protocol.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review IDQ related services after the upgrade to make sure they are up and running.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the IDS upgrade process?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div><br /></div>
